Taxpayers' Association Actively Protests the Assessment of Rent for Collection of General Rates 128

In the future, the general rates will inevitably be greater than the rent one day

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession is protesting the Municipal Council's destruction of municipal principles. It is reported that the assessment of rent for the collection of general rates has actually increased the rate from 1% to 20%. The entire city is unanimously opposed to the Municipal Council, but there has been no concrete response. The following is the letter from the Taxpayers' Association to the Municipal Council:

Taxpayers' Association to the Municipal Council: We are writing in response to the letter from the Shanghai Zhongshe (see yesterday's newspaper), which included a draft letter, certificate, lease, rent receipt, etc. Upon investigation, the association believes that your council's act of destroying municipal financial principles by assessing rent for the collection of general rates and actually increasing the rate is inappropriate and should be corrected. We have repeatedly sent letters to this effect. We hereby request that you investigate and handle the case, and promptly cancel the action of increasing the rate, so as to avoid causing major disputes. To the Municipal Council.

Taxpayers' Association to Zhongshe: We are writing in response to your letter of today, regarding the Municipal Council's assessment of rent for the collection of general rates, which is equivalent to a huge increase in the rate, and requesting negotiations. The attachments have been received. The association has repeatedly reported this matter and sent letters to the Municipal Council requesting the cancellation of this measure, which is inconsistent with municipal financial principles. We have learned that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Preparatory Committee of the Citizens' Association of the Special District have also sent letters to the Municipal Council making the same claim. In the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, the association actively protested the Municipal Council's increase of the police rate by two li from the autumn of that year for the benefit of all taxpayers. The increase in the police rate calculated by the Municipal Council based on the estimated rent is far more than two li. As your association stated, it has increased from 4% to over 20%. According to our knowledge, it has even increased from 1.4% to over 26%. If this bad precedent is set, there will inevitably be a day when the police rate is greater than the rent. Will taxpayers still have the ability to bear the burden? In addition to sending a letter to the Municipal Council, we hereby reply for your information. The attachments are temporarily stored here. To Shanghai Zhongshe.

Discussing the Year-End Closing Period 129

All ports should follow the lead of Shanghai's Qian Industry

Since the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau proposed the year-end closing period for industrial and commercial accounting in the twentieth year and solicited opinions from various industries, the Shanghai Qian Industry unanimously agreed that the end of January of the following year was the most appropriate. After sending letters to various port industry associations, they have recently received letters from various port industry associations unanimously agreeing. In addition to the letters from the Nanjing and Wuhu Qian Industry Associations that were published in yesterday's newspaper, we have now obtained five more letters from Nantong, Jiangdu, Jiujiang, Qingdao, and Yingkou, which are reproduced below:

Nantong Qian Industry Association: Upon receiving your letter and attachments, we greatly admire your foresight in setting the year-end closing period for the twentieth year at the end of January and advocating for its adoption. We should unanimously support it to achieve the goal. We have already transcribed the message to various industries to jointly strive for it. In addition to writing an article based on the intention of your esteemed association and requesting the county chamber of commerce to forward it to the Executive Yuan and ministries, we still hope for your guidance at any time.

Jiangdu Qian Industry Association: Upon receiving your letter requesting to determine the national industrial and commercial accounting year, and based on the proposal of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to set the end of February as the year-end closing period and sending letters to various industry associations to solicit opinions, the association convened a general meeting of all members to discuss it in detail. The members unanimously agreed that setting the end of February as the year-end closing period has various obstacles and advocated that setting the end of January as the year-end closing period is the most appropriate. This has been unanimously approved and the reasons have been detailed in a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce requesting its adoption. After receiving your esteemed letter, the association immediately convened a general meeting of all members to discuss it. The members unanimously stated that the proposal of your esteemed association is very insightful and not only benefits the Qian Industry but also benefits commerce and agriculture. This is especially admired by our colleagues. In addition to informing the county chamber of commerce, we hereby send a special letter to express our association's agreement.

Jiujiang Qian Industry Association: Upon receiving your letter of the thirteenth and three drafts, we are fully aware of everything. Regarding the so-called end of January as the year-end closing period, the association immediately convened a general meeting of all members for discussion. They all agreed and believed that setting the end of January as the year-end closing period is indeed appropriate. Since your esteemed association has sent a letter to the government and various agencies requesting it, our association is determined to unanimously support and strive for it and is willing to be your backer.

Qingdao Qian Industry Association: Upon receiving your esteemed letter, we respectfully listened to all the proposed methods for closing the accounts. The difficulties you described are accurate and relevant to the situation in Qingdao. After reading it, we greatly admire it. Our colleagues express great sympathy for the views of your esteemed association and unanimously approve and are willing to follow your great example and take consistent steps and remotely support your esteemed association in order to achieve the goal. We hope that your esteemed association will continue to proceed for the benefit of our Qian Industry.

Yingkou Qian Industry Association: Upon receiving your letter and attachments, we are fully aware of everything. The association convened a general meeting of all members for discussion. The members unanimously agreed that the commercial conditions in the north and south are generally the same, and setting the end of January as the year-end closing period is considered the most appropriate, which is consistent with the proposal of your esteemed association. We hereby reply for your information and hope that you will actively proceed so that it can be realized as soon as possible.

News of the Dissolution of the National Pharmaceutical Federation 130

Remarks by Zhang Meian, Standing Committee Member

The National Federation of Pharmaceutical Organizations of this city was previously dissolved by the 131st Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Government. According to Mr. Zhang Meian, a standing committee member of the association, the news of the association's dissolution was only seen in the Central Government's resolution of the 131st Standing Committee Meeting published in the local newspapers on March 6th. However, as of today, the Central Government has not yet sent a clear order of dissolution to the association. However, since the Central Government has made a resolution to dissolve it, the association should comply with it. Therefore, the association has already resolved at a standing committee meeting to prepare for dissolution. Once the clear order arrives, work can be stopped. However, the pharmaceutical organizations under the association are located throughout the country, and there are also many branches overseas. The association is jointly organized by the medical, pharmaceutical, and labor sectors nationwide. When the organization was initially established, it was intended to concentrate efforts to jointly develop the pharmaceutical industry, so the cooperation of the medical, pharmaceutical, and labor sectors was painstakingly constructed. Now that the association has been ordered to dissolve, the branches in various provinces, cities, and counties will of course be dissolved uniformly, and the spirit of cooperation between the medical, pharmaceutical, and labor sectors will be fundamentally eliminated. This is regrettable. However, the reason why the Central Government is dissolving the association this time is precisely because it has violated the organizational regulations of people's organizations by mixing the medical, pharmaceutical, and labor sectors. The country's legislation is such, and the association should obey the decision of the Central Government. As for the national medical and pharmaceutical sectors after the association is dissolved, they can continue the spirit of the past and implement unity in accordance with the law. However, medicine and pharmaceuticals are different paths and should go their separate ways. When the Central National Medicine Hall held a preparatory conference in the capital last month, many representatives of medical and pharmaceutical organizations from various places went to Beijing to attend. During the interval, they made a detailed discussion on the issue of the association's dissolution. As a result, the majority advocated that after the association is dissolved, the medical side should follow the example of the National Physicians' Association and the medical colleagues in various places should initiate the organization of the National Chinese Medicine Federation. The pharmaceutical side should follow the regulations of the industry and commerce guild law and the pharmaceutical colleagues in various places should initiate the organization of the National Chinese Medicine Guild Federation. In the future, the two associations will be located in one place and can still contact each other for handling matters. This plan meets the needs and complies with the laws and regulations. If it can be realized, then even though the association is dissolved, it will not have any impact on the entire national Chinese medicine. The Central Government will definitely approve the establishment without any doubt. Tracing back to the establishment of the association on March 17th of the eighteenth year, it first passed the abolition of Chinese medicine case with the Central Health Committee and fought against it with all its strength. Finally, relying on the efforts of colleagues nationwide, it won the sympathy of people from all walks of life and fundamentally abolished this bill. The following year, the Ministry of Health and the Ministry of Education issued orders prohibiting Chinese medicine from establishing schools, Chinese medicine from establishing hospitals, and Chinese medicine from using Western instruments and methods to treat people's diseases. Regarding the pharmaceutical aspect, there were also so-called regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants. In essence, all of its contents were sufficient to fetter the future development of China's medical and pharmaceutical industry. The harm to China's medical and pharmaceutical community in this environment is unspeakable. Subsequently, the association convened the Second National Congress of Medical and Pharmaceutical Organizations. It was unanimously resolved in Shanghai to nominate myself and Mr. Qiu Jisheng to go to Beijing to petition. Fortunately, Chairman Chiang was wise and decisive and immediately issued a handwritten instruction to abolish the ordinances that imprisoned Chinese medicine and pharmaceuticals. Thus, the Chinese medicine and pharmaceuticals that were on the verge of death had a chance to survive. However, the association was still worried that the status of national medicine and pharmaceuticals could not be consolidated. It also requested the Executive Yuan to follow the example of the National Health Hall and prepare to establish the Central National Medicine Hall as the hub for the revitalization of Chinese medicine and pharmaceuticals. It also relied on the assistance of the late President Tan and the Central Committee members Chen Lifu and Jiao Yitang to submit it to the Central Political Conference for approval to establish it. Now the Central National Medicine Hall has been established by advanced party and state officials. The task of the association can be completed. Counting the past work of the association, although there has not been much achievement, it has fortunately avoided the danger of falling. This is what all colleagues of the association can tell the medical and pharmaceutical colleagues nationwide.

Invoices Issued by Stores Should Be Stamped 131

All those over one yuan should be stamped with one cent

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to various industries in this city through the industry association yesterday, stating that on the 30th of this month, it received a letter from the Shanghai Special Zone Stamp Tax Office of the Jiangsu Stamp Alcohol and Tobacco Tax Bureau, stating that the Chinese Chemical Industry Corporation had stated in its letter that invoices issued by stores are different in nature from silver and money documents and should be exempt from stamping. Please explain so that it can be followed, etc. Accordingly, the office replied that invoices are certificates for urging payment of debts. According to social customs, when a debt is received, a receipt is not issued separately. Therefore, they are stamped separately according to the silver and money receipts. Later, an order was received from the Ministry of Finance that in order to show consideration for the hardships of merchants, all foreign amounts above one yuan should be stamped with one cent and no additional stamps should be affixed. This has been followed for a long time. Before the revised Stamp Tax Law is promulgated, it should still be handled according to the original plan. In view of the foregoing, a letter is hereby issued to inform you so that you can follow it.

A Jinghu Locomotive Derailed Yesterday 136

Passenger trains delayed

At 1:30 p.m. yesterday, the No. 34 locomotive on the Jinghu Railway was sending eight coal cars to the coal yard road when the foremost car suddenly fell into the track at a junction, blocking the tracks. Since the location was also the entrance and exit for cars on the Jinghu, Hangzhou, and Ningbo lines, the train to Beijing from the gate, as well as the Shanghai-Changzhou, Shanghai-Wuxi, and Hangzhou No. 8 express trains and the No. 10 Beijing-Hangzhou trains, were all detained at the North Station and could not depart on time. The workers from the engine factory immediately tried to empty the coal cars and put them back on the tracks. It was not until about 6:40 p.m. that the tracks were cleared and the trains were able to depart. Each train was delayed for more than an hour.

Although there are minor issues, they are not a problem

From tonight onwards, they should be closed. However, due to environmental inconveniences, it cannot stop dog racing on its own. Therefore, unless the Municipal Council takes active measures to interfere, it will continue to race dogs. It is scheduled to hold races as usual this Saturday. However, if the Municipal Council starts negotiations to resolve the issue at this time, the association is willing to postpone it indefinitely. In addition, it is heard that Mingyuan has signed numerous contracts with employees and other related parties. The Debt of the Riye Bank Has Not Yet Been Distributed 140

Greatly Different from What Was Said in Yesterday's Newspaper

There Is Still Hope for Full Repayment in the Future

Directors Must Advance at Least 20% in Cash

The Sale of Shops Is Progressing Actively

Yesterday, this newspaper reported on the case of the Riye Bank liquidation heard by the Mixed Court of the French Concession, stating that accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang, among others, claimed that lawsuits had been filed against those who had not repaid their debts to various accounts, and that many had already been repaid, allowing for a preliminary distribution of 20% to each creditor. Upon investigation, this information does not match the facts. It was found that what accountants Wu and Pan said at the time was that, although the pursuit of debts from various accounts was actively underway, the estimated total debt of the company was significantly different from what was needed to fully repay all debts. Therefore, they requested the court to order the shareholders and directors of the company to advance at least 20% in cash so that distribution could be made as soon as possible, not that there was already sufficient money available for a preliminary distribution of 20%.

According to another report, since the French Concession court appointed accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang to liquidate the Riye Bank, they have been actively pursuing debts and selling off various institutions affiliated with the Gongfa Company. Yesterday, someone met with accountants Wu and Pan to inquire about the progress of future debt repayment. They said that most of the debts owed to the Riye Bank were related to the Gongfa Company and Huang Chujiu, making it particularly difficult to recover them. As of yesterday, only a little over 40,000 yuan had been received in scattered payments. The Chinese and Western pharmacy was sold for 240,000 yuan, but the deposit had not yet been paid. The hot spring bathhouse was sold for 50,000 yuan, but the deal had not been finalized due to rental issues. Even if the above two deals could be completed and added to the scattered payments received, it would still be difficult to distribute even 10%. Yesterday's report mentioned a 20% distribution, but that is not yet possible. As for future repayment plans, efforts must be made to fully repay the creditors, as the creditors of the bank are mostly women and laborers. It is currently planned to sell off each of the Gongfa Company's shops one by one and auction off Huang Chujiu's estate. If that is not enough, a request will be submitted to the French Concession court to order the shareholders and directors to pursue repayment.

Communist Organization Smashed in the French Concession 141

Communist Books Seized

The French police recently discovered that individuals were secretly establishing Communist organizations at No. 5 Anshun Lane, Kangti Road, Xinxin Lane, Jin Shenfu Road, and No. 4 Weiyuan Lane, Lafayette Road. Numerous Communist books were seized. They were taken to the police station, interrogated by the chief detective, and ordered to be detained for further investigation. It is scheduled to be sent to the French Concession court for interrogation today.

Bandit Leader Wang Zhixiang Sentenced to Death 142

Bandit leader Wang Zhixiang (also known as Wang Haixiang and Wang Biezui) from Ningbo was arrested by Chinese detective Wang Changgen and Bao detective Wang Yingjie of the Laozha police station. He confessed to being involved in the kidnapping of prominent businessmen Bei Runsheng, Shi Jiufeng, Liang Huibao, He Fangpu, and Wu Songyan. Subsequently, the police lawyer Ru Bao-yi filed a public prosecution, requesting that he be sentenced to the most severe punishment according to the law. After repeated hearings and deliberations by the Special District Court, the date for the verdict was reached yesterday morning. The police brought the defendant to court, where Judge Zhou Han of the Criminal Court announced the verdict, sentencing the defendant Wang Zhixiang to death for each of the two counts of jointly kidnapping and extorting ransom, and ordering the execution of the death penalty. The remaining charges were acquitted.

Case of Three Lawyers Being Sued 143

Examined by Judge Feng Yesterday

Lawyer Zhang Xingyuan Did Not Arrive

The Plaintiff Could Not Speak the Shanghai Dialect

Postponed to Saturday for Further Hearing

The Guangdong woman Zheng Lanru, residing on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, filed a criminal lawsuit in the Special District Court against lawyers Huang Shaochang, Gao Hanqiao, and Zhang Xingyuan, accusing them of perjury and fraud. The Special Court scheduled the trial for March 31, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the date for the trial arrived. Defendants Huang and Gao, as well as the plaintiff, arrived in turn. However, Zhang Xingheng alone did not arrive. Judge Feng Shide ascended to the Fifth Court. Due to the time spent examining other cases, this case was not addressed until the clock struck five. Furthermore, the plaintiff, Zheng Lanru, could only speak the Yue dialect, making it difficult for the judge to understand. An interpreter was needed, but the interpreters familiar with the Yue dialect in the court had already left work and returned home, so the examination could not proceed. Judge Feng then ordered that the examination be postponed to Saturday afternoon of this week.

Verdict Announced in the Case of Tenants in Qingyun Lane Being Sued 144

Rent Owed Must Be Paid in Full

The Request for Eviction Was Rejected

The British firm New Sassoon & Co. previously filed a civil lawsuit in the Special District Court against 164 tenants, including Gan Taixing, in Qingyun Lane, claiming that they were occupying the premises without paying rent and requesting an order for their eviction to facilitate reconstruction and to recover the rent owed. Judge Zhou Daren of the Civil Court took on the case and began arguments on the 23rd of last month. The plaintiff's agent, H.P. Maine, and two foreign lawyers elaborated on the plaintiff's reasons for demolishing the houses for reconstruction. The tenants' lawyers, Xue Jiaqi and Wang Zuxun, refuted the legality of the plaintiff's demolition activities based on legal principles. After lengthy and eloquent arguments on both sides, the verdict was scheduled for 9:00 AM on March 31. Yesterday was the date for the verdict. At 9:00 AM, Judge Zhou ascended to the court and announced the main text of the verdict: "The plaintiff, New Sassoon & Co., sued the tenants of Qingyun Lane, including Gan Taixing, for owing rent in the amount of a certain number of houses. The tenants of each house should pay the rent owed in full. The plaintiff's request for an order for the tenants to vacate is rejected and will be transferred to the mediation court for reconciliation." After the judgment was pronounced, the court adjourned.

Establishment of an Office for Protecting Coastal Fisheries Outside Songkou 145

This Year's Fishing Season Has Arrived. The Various Gangs of Pirates Outside Wusongkou Are Still Rampant, Forcing Fishermen to Pay Contributions, Causing Fishermen's Ships Not to Dare to Set Sail. Furthermore, the Spring Fishing Season is an Important Livelihood for Fishermen Throughout the Year. Representatives Were Immediately Sent to the Province to Petition. The Provincial Government Has Conjointly Established an Office for Protecting Coastal Fisheries with the Jiangsu Pacification Superintendent and the Coast Guard of the Navy Department Outside Wusongkou. Zhang's House in Tongshu Hengfu Lane Has Been Surveyed and Equipped with a Small Shortwave Radio. The Formation of an Offshore Patrol Team is Underway, Rotating Patrols on the Ocean Surface. In the Meantime, All Fishing Boats Have Been Notified to Set Sail Early to Catch Fish to Avoid Losses from the Spring Fishing Season.

Underwear Company Returns Savings Deposits 147

Since the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Ordered the Ban on Stores Running Savings Operations Concurrently, Limiting Their Closure to One Month, the Underwear Company Reported and Announced a One-Month Suspension Due to the Abrupt Nature of the Event and the Short Deadline, as the Collected Savings Deposits, Apart from a Small Amount of Reserves, Had All Been Converted into Inventory and Machinery. It Is Reported That the Company Has Now Set April 1st as the Starting Date for Returning Savings Deposits, as Follows: (1) "Current Deposits" Can Be Withdrawn at Any Time, with Interest Calculated Up to the Date of Payment. (2) "Lump-Sum Savings" Will Be Repaid in Full at a Weekly Interest Rate of 9%. (3) Other "Time Deposits" Will Be Withdrawn Upon Maturity in Accordance with the Regulations. The Notice Has Already Been Given to All Depositors.

Completion of the New Songhu Railway Station 148

Relocation Still Pending

Since the Songhu Railway Began Using Steam-Powered Automatic Locomotives in April of Last Year, the Baoshan Road Barrier Gate Has Been Constantly Opened and Closed, Causing Inconvenience to Pedestrians and Vehicles. At the Request of the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Railway Bureau Began Construction of a New Station on the East End of Baoshan Road Last Month, the Details of Which Have Been Repeatedly Reported in This Newspaper. It Is Reported That the Construction of the New Station Has Progressed Extremely Rapidly, and All Facilities Such As the Station Ticket Office, Waiting Room, Platform, Coal Platform, Canopy, Iron Fence, and Road Surface Have Been Completed. The Railway Bureau Originally Planned to Have Vehicles Stop at the Station to Pick Up and Drop Off Passengers Starting on April 1st (Today). However, After the Bureau Sent Personnel to Survey the New Station Project, It Was Discovered That the Station Platform Needed to Be Lengthened and That the Location of the Coal Platform Was Quite Inappropriate and Also Needed to Be Moved. Therefore, It Is Necessary to Wait Until the Above Projects Are Completed Before Moving to the New Station to Conduct Business.

Discussion on the Issue of Tobacco and Alcohol License Taxes

Previously, the License Tax Affairs for Tobacco and Alcohol Merchants in the Chinese Area Were Handled by Outsiders, Entirely for Profit. The Allotments Increased Year by Year, Monopolizing the Operations and Exploiting Fellow Traders, Causing Long-Term Suffering. The Two Associations of the Industry Have Repeatedly Convened Joint Meetings. A General Representative Meeting of the Tobacco and Alcohol Industries Was Held at 2:00 PM Yesterday at No. 357 Ningbo Road, the Tobacco Exchange Industry Association. An Accountant Arrived with Over Forty People from the Soy Sauce and Alcohol Industry and Over Thirty People from the Tobacco Exchange Industry. Zhu Sirong and Seven Others Represented Zheng Yatang and Seventy Others. Chen Liangyu Was Unanimously Elected Chairman to Report on the Progress of the Situation. After Discussion, It Was Publicly Decided to First Send a Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for Assistance and to Designate Cheng Gengli, Fan Dongsheng, Chen Weiwen, Zhang Baokang, Chen Liangyu, Shen Weiting, Qian Wenda, and Wang Chengchen as Eight Representatives to Take the Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for Delivery. Important Decisions Were Made on Two Cases: (1) The Tax Was Approved to Be Handled Publicly by the Two Industries Requesting the Association to Request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Report the Situation to the Ministry of Finance and the Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau to Avoid Manipulation. (2) If the Tax Is Still Handled by Contractors, the Two Industries Will Formulate Other Measures and Vow Not to Recognize It. The Meeting Unanimously Approved It and Adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Proclamation Banning the Live Plucking of Pig Bristles 152

A Fine of Five Silver Dollars Per Head

Proclamation by the Municipal Public Security and Health Bureaus: In the Matter of a Proclamation, the Municipal Government Instructed That, Based on the Petition Submitted by Chen Yuexing, a Pig Slaughtering Representative, and He Rusheng, et Al., on Behalf of Changhe and Other Pig Pens, Regarding the Live Plucking of Pig Bristles Disrupting Business, We Request That the Bureau Investigate and Ban the Practice. We Are Jointly Investigating and Prohibiting This. Furthermore, This Health Bureau Also Received a Petition from Pig Slaughtering Representative He Rusheng and the Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association, Echoing the Previous Situation, Stating That the Banning of the Private Plucking of Live Pig Bristles Had Already Been Proclaimed. Now, Five Provisions for the Banning Measures Are Specifically Stipulated. Hereafter, If Any Live Pig Bristles Are Plucked, Once Discovered or Reported, the Offenders Will Be Punished According to the Prescribed Measures Without Lenience. In Addition to Reporting to the Municipal Government for Record, This Proclamation Is Being Issued for General Knowledge. All Must Abide by It Without Violation.

Measures for Banning the Private Plucking of Live Pig Bristles: (1) Those Found to Be Live Plucking Pig Bristles Will Be Fined Five Silver Dollars Per Head Based on the Number of Pigs Plucked, or Detained for Five Days, and the Plucked Bristles Will Be Confiscated Entirely and Executed by the Public Security Bureau in the Responsible Area. (2) When Sand Boats, Steamships, and Trains Transporting Pigs Arrive in Shanghai, If Pigs Without Bristles Are Found, the Recipient Designated by the Pig Pen or Pig Bank Must Not Receive These Pigs Without Bristles and Must Jointly Investigate and Verify the Number of Pigs with Bristles Removed with the Pig Carriers and Send the Perpetrator of the Private Plucking of Live Pig Bristles to the Nearest Area Office of the Public Security Bureau for Punishment in Accordance with Article 1 Before the Pigs Can Be Transported into the Pen. (3) If the Bristles of Pigs Are Plucked in the Lighters, the Owner of the Pig Bank and the Ship Owner Should Be Responsible for Investigating and Verifying the Number of Pigs with Bristles Removed and Send the Workers on the Lighter Who Private Plucked the Pig Bristles to the Nearest Area Office of the Public Security Bureau for Punishment in Accordance with Article 1 Before the Pigs Can Be Transported into the Pen. (4) If the Bristles of Pigs Are Plucked in the Pen, the Pen Owner Should Be Responsible for Investigating and Verifying the Number of Pigs with Bristles Removed and Send the Perpetrator of the Private Plucking of Pig Bristles to the Nearest Area Office of the Public Security Bureau for Punishment in Accordance with Article 1 Before the Pigs Are Allowed to Be Transported out of the Pen. (5) If There Is a Violation of the Provisions of Articles 2, 3, and 4, Once Discovered, the Fine Set Forth in Article 1 Will Be Doubled (March 31, Year 20).

Coffin Prices Increase 156

Since Qin Yanqi and Zhu Cisheng Took Over as Director and Deputy Director of the Shanghai Charity Association Tongren Fuyuan Hall, They Have Seriously Rectified the Affairs of Various Departments, Which Are Gradually Coming into Order. The Hall Has Been Offering Coffins for Sale on Credit, Originally to Facilitate Citizens and as a Charitable Undertaking. There Are Eight Types of Coffins: Wealth, Prosperity, Longevity, Happiness, Celebration, Regular, Deputy, and General. They Are All Sold at the Actual Cost of the Materials and Labor for Making the Coffins, Without Taking Any Profit. Recently, Due to the Sharp Rise in Lumber Prices and the Increase in Labor and Materials Costs, Selling at the Original Prices Is Not Enough to Cover the Costs. The Board of Directors of the Charity Association Has Resolved to Appropriately Increase the Prices. Except for the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall on Avenue Ningbo in the Concession, Which Is Selling at Actual Prices with Lower Subsidies, the Main Hall Will Still Have a Semi-Credit System for the Regular, Deputy, and General Coffins. Based on a Comparison of Last Year's Credit Amounts, More Than Ten Thousand Jin Will Still Need to Be Subsidized Annually. Therefore, New Coffin Prices Have Been Set to Maintain the Cost, Effective from the First Day of This Month. The Prices of Each Type of Coffin Are Recorded Below: Wealth, 126 Yuan; Prosperity, 110 Yuan; Longevity, 80 Yuan; Happiness, 66 Yuan; Celebration, 54 Yuan; Regular, 32 Yuan; Deputy, 20 Yuan; General, 16 Yuan.

Flour Boat Collides with Charcoal Boat 160

Boat Pierced, People Fall into Water

The Yongchengxiang Company, Hired by Zhuang Ke from Zhejiang's Jiahu to Ship Goods to Shanghai, Hired Ruan Bao-kui's Boat to Carry 500 Bags of Flour and North-South Goods, Salted Fish, and Other Goods Worth Over 10,000 Taels of Silver to Huzhou for Delivery. The Boat Set Sail the Day Before Yesterday Afternoon. Due to the Tide, It Anchored Overnight in Longhua Bay. At Approximately 5:00 AM Yesterday Morning, It Raised Anchor and Sailed with the Wind. However, When Sailing in the Lujiaya Pu Area, the Wind Was Unfavorable. The Boatswain Turned the Rudder to Veer, But the Rudder Was Turned Too Late, and the Boat Collided with Feng Sanguan's Ningbo Charcoal Boat Anchored on the Edge of the Pu. After the Collision, the Bow of Ruan's Boat Was Shattered, and the Cargo Was Very Heavy, Causing the Boat to Sink Immediately and the Crew to Fall into the Water. Feng's Boat Was Also Hit with a Foot-Long Hole, and Many Baskets of Charcoal on the Deck Were Knocked Off. The Oar Was Also Knocked into the Water. Feng's Boat Lowered a Sampan to Rescue the People. They Rescued a Steersman and One of Ruan's Crew Members. Two Crew Members of Ruan's Boat Could Not Be Rescued. Feng Has Now Detained Ruan to Negotiate Compensation for Losses. Ruan Sent Crew Members to Shanghai to Report to Yongchengxiang. Fortunately, the Cargo Was Insured for Water Damage. The Company Immediately Reported to the Company and Took a Small Wheelbarrow to the Scene of the Accident to Investigate the Collision. Ruan's Boat Sank. Fortunately, It Was in a Shallow Place, and the Boat Was Exposed Above the Water. The Company Has Hired a Wheelbarrow to Find a Way to Salvage the Sunken Boat, But It Will Be Very Costly and Is Still Being Discussed. Ruan Was Detained by Feng to Claim Compensation for Losses, Which Is Temporarily the Responsibility of the Company, So Ruan Escaped and Returned to Shanghai.

Restaurant Worker Burned

Resolution of Disputes between Two Steamers 162

The Public Harmony Steamer of Jardine Matheson & Co. After the Major Dispute between the Old and New Stewards Last Time, the Seamen's Union Made Representations to Jardine Matheson and Others, and the Two Sides Discussed It Many Times. It Was Not Until Yesterday That It Came to an End. Jardine Matheson & Co. Has Approved the Resignation of the Comprador Shen Huating and Appointed Chen Bainian as His Successor. Yesterday, Chen Arrived at the Trade Union and Discussed the Solution with the Trade Union and Worker Representatives. (1) The New Comprador Will Not Collect Guarantee Money or Meal Money from the Workers. (2) Members of the Seamen's Union Will Be Used as Before. (3) The Guarantee Money of 38 Non-Seamen's Union Members Working in the Boat's Hold Will Be Returned, and They Will All Be Dismissed from the Boat. (4) The Comprador Will Not Add New Workers, Only Bring One Attendant, Who Will Leave the Boat at the Same Time When He Leaves His Post. The Above Provisions of the Agreement Were Signed by Zhao Zhizhi, Representative of the General Seamen's Union, He Zhenhuan, Representative of the Shanghai Branch, Yang Guisheng, Worker Representative, Zhou Xiaoting, Representative of the Middle Cabin Guild, and Chen Bainian, the Comprador. Thus, a Dispute Came to an End.

China Bank Inspection Report 164

Report No. 37

The 37th inspection report of the Shanghai China Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee stated that the committee members and entrusted accountants, based on the rules of the committee, inspected the issuance and interbank exchange coupon reserve vault of the Shanghai China Bank headquarters on March 29th of the 20th year of the Republic of China. The Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance also joined the inspection. The results of the inspection are listed below: The total amount of exchange coupons issued was 12,188,938.89 yuan, including 62,091,283 yuan issued by the headquarters, 27,266,282 yuan used by interbank branches, and 32,531,824 yuan used by various banks and firms. Except for the portion used by various banks and firms, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection focuses on the interbank portion, as follows: The amount issued by the headquarters and used by interbank branches is 89,357,565 yuan. The reserve amount for exchange coupons in the headquarters and interbank branches is 89,357,565 yuan, including 54,169,757.95 yuan in cash reserve and 35,187,807.05 yuan in guarantee reserve. The above two items total six-tenths in cash reserve and four-tenths in guarantee reserve, both of which were checked without error. In accordance with Article 5 of the rules, this is a formal report. March 29th, the 20th year of the Republic of China. Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance Xu Kan, Representatives of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Pei Yunqing and Wang Yansong, Representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association Ye Fuxiao and Wu Yunzhai, Representatives of the Shanghai Money Trade Association Xie Taofu and Pei Yunqing, Representatives of Coupon-Receiving Banks and Firms Yang Dunfu and Luo Zhiyun, Representatives of the Board of Directors and Supervisors of the China Bank Ye Zhuotang, Zhou Zongliang, Xu Jiqing, and Li Zhiyun, Accountant Wang Zikang.

Lodger Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium 167

The day before yesterday evening, a man claiming to be Xu Lianwu from Shanxi, approximately 30 years old, checked into a room alone at a certain hotel on the east end of Baoxing Lane on Avenue Edward VII. For unknown reasons, driven by a pessimistic outlook, he committed suicide by swallowing raw opium. Yesterday morning, the tea boy knocked on his door, and when there was no response, he forced the door open and entered the room. Xu had already died, with opium residue around his mouth. The tea boy immediately reported it to the police station, who sent detectives to investigate. They found a letter in his pocket written on stationery from the Tongshi Wen Accountant Firm, with the envelope addressed to Mr. Jiang at Kua Long Road, Da Nan Men, Shanghai. There was nothing else. The letter appeared to be a returned express mail. The body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for an autopsy. Since no relatives were found, the case is awaiting investigation.

Chen Gusheng Commits Suicide for Daughter 168

Chen Gusheng's eldest daughter, A Lin, returned home with her mother and daughter the day before yesterday because Chen did not allow her to return home. This infuriated Chen, leading him to commit suicide. At 4:20 PM yesterday afternoon, he locked himself in his bedroom and used scissors to stab his throat, severing his trachea. He died instantly. The local bailiff reported the incident to the court for investigation. At 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, Prosecutor Wu Deying, accompanied by an autopsy officer and bailiffs, went to investigate and confirmed the suicide. The family prepared a coffin for burial.

Trade Associations Must Register Before Establishment 170

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a notice yesterday to all trade associations, stating: "Regarding the matter of the application for registration by the Shanghai Department Store Trade Association, this Chamber previously received instructions from the Bureau of Social Affairs stating that the association had not followed Article 2 of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Group Registration Regulations by submitting an application for registration to the Bureau. Therefore, the request for registration cannot be processed until the aforementioned registration procedures are completed. The association stated that Article 2 of the registration regulations requires the submission of an application form co-signed by the initiators, resumes of the preparatory committee members, and the permit from the City Party Headquarters, as well as the preparatory committee's seal impression, which is difficult to comply with. The association requested an exemption. This Chamber forwarded the situation to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs for instructions. The Bureau's reply, No. 8006, stated that, 'Having received and understood the report, it is proven that the association has difficulty completing the registration procedures. Therefore, temporary leniency is granted for handling the matter. However, in the future, any newly organized trade association preparatory committees within the city that have obtained a permit from the Municipal People's Training Committee but have not submitted the procedures for registration in accordance with Article 2 of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Group Registration Regulations will not be assigned personnel to supervise the election during the inaugural meeting. All committee members elected at that time will be deemed invalid. You are instructed to ensure that all subordinates pay attention to this matter.' This Chamber hereby issues this notice for your information and compliance."

Advance Sale of "Collected Works of Old Beijing" 172

Sun Shi Zheng, Grand Historian of Changshu, was a prominent figure in the literary circles of his time, excelling in poetry and prose. His writing is comparable to that of Wang Xizhi and Gui Youguang. It is now reported that Sun's "Collected Works of Old Beijing," consisting of eight volumes of essays and eight volumes of poems, has been printed in movable type in Beijing and is currently being bound. It has taken more than half a year to complete. The quality of the publication is unparalleled. After entering the Hanlin Academy during the late Qing Dynasty, Sun's literary reputation soared, and he was appreciated by Weng Tonghe, Zhang Zhidong, and others. Many prominent literary figures and officials of today have been his students. Zhang Xueliang, Deputy Commander of Liaoning, admired his talent and specially invited him to compile the "General Gazetteer of the Three Provinces." Recently, due to financial difficulties, he published his works to earn a living. He is one of the three "old men who live by selling their writings," along with Fan Fanshan and Bao Ruichen. All scholars admire him. It is now reported that Sun, to favor the poor scholars, is offering an advance sale. The combined price for the collection of poems and essays is six yuan, and the advance sale price is three yuan, which only covers the cost of paper and ink. However, a minimum purchase of five sets is required. Postage is an additional 5%. For every ten sets purchased, a copy of "Reading Classics to Save the Country," "Poetry History Pavilion Series," "Birthday Poems of Famous People," and "Ren-Gui Poetry Collection" will be added as a gift. For every five sets purchased, a copy of "Poetry History Pavilion Series" and "Ren-Gui Poetry Collection" will be added... It is reported that more than three hundred people have already placed orders. The address for purchase is Sun's residence at No. 38 Xizhuan Hutong, Xuanwumenwai, Beijing.

Meeting of the Gold and Silver Industry Across the Province 173

There are no fewer than a hundred or so gold and silversmiths in this city. Since the provincial government drafted a business tax rate of 10 per mille, the industry is extremely concerned and is jointly seeking ways to reduce it. Yesterday, representatives from Suzhou, Zhenjiang, Yangzhou, Nanjing, Wuxi, Taizhou, Kunshan, and other places arrived in Shanghai, all unanimously advocating for a reduction in the business tax rate. Therefore, the Shanghai Trade Association held a joint meeting to decide that, due to the different jurisdictions, the first step would be for Shanghai to petition the Shanghai Municipal Government, and for the counties to jointly petition the provincial government, in order to achieve a unified approach.

World Anecdotes 177

— Hai Ke

▲In the Hebrides, a group of islands west of northern Scotland, there is an island called Lewis. Stornoway, the main town on the island, is full of beautiful villas and women wearing the most fashionable European clothes. However, the people in the interior of the island do not even understand English and become suspicious when they see foreigners. They are completely like an uncivilized race.

▲There are several underground rivers in London, one of which is called the Tigris. It is said that it was originally a ditch that was widened by the ancient Danish king Canute to allow Danish ships to sail in and surround the fortresses around the Thames to Kennington.

▲Recently, in England, in order to test the air at high altitudes, three people were locked in a barrel 15 feet long and 9 feet in diameter. Later, they felt the air gradually thinning, as if they were at an altitude of 27,888 feet, and the temperature was abnormally cold at 22 degrees below zero.

▲In one of the very large wheat stacks owned by the Australian British government, countless dead rats were once found. Later, they were collected together and weighed, totaling eight tons.

▲There are many factories in London, and the amount of coal ash that falls each year is 369 tons per square mile.

Today's Words 178

— Chen Boying

What day is today if not April 1st? This day is no different from any other day of the month in our country. However, in France, it is a strange day. What is strange? It is that everyone can lie on this day. The origin of lying is said to be that Jesus lied to escape from difficulties on April 1st, and later generations commemorated Jesus by designating this day as a day for lying. Therefore, on this day, one can deceive others and be deceived by others. It is said that one person met a friend on the road, and the friend said that the neighbor was careless and that their house would be affected. The person hurried home, but everything was fine, so he realized he had been deceived. Another person planned how to fool an acquaintance after leaving home. He met a friend who was walking in a hurry. When asked where he was going, he said that he had important business. He also said that he would have dinner at a famous restaurant in two hours and invited the person to go with him. The person agreed, and the friend hurried away. When the time came, he went to look for his friend but could not find him, and he realized that he had been deceived. Others may invite guests on behalf of someone, but the host had not made such an invitation; or they may make an appointment but not find the place; or they may order something that is not urgent. These are all castles in the air, focusing on the unreal and neglecting the real. I think that on this day, everyone should pay attention to the words of others, which actually contain a lesson. Also, throughout the year, people always say serious things. It is especially interesting to have one day when one can break free from the shackles of honesty and escape from the norm, without causing any harm. The world may have people who enjoy this and make every day like April 1st, but that is beyond my knowledge.

Interesting Facts from the Half-Yearly Meeting of the Child Welfare Association 183

— Sun Choucheng

The Chinese Child Welfare Association is jointly established by Chinese and American educators, collecting donations to promote the happiness of children. The half-yearly members' meeting was held at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce on Saturday (the 28th). Half of the members who attended were Chinese and half were Westerners. In addition to reporting on the association's affairs in the past half-year, famous people were invited to give speeches. Here are some interesting excerpts from the meeting:

On this day, the association's order sheets and other materials were all in light green, which was different from the usual white used in meetings. It is said that doctors value the color green, and the association is charitable and dedicated to educating poor children, so it adopted this color. Dozens of photos of children when they were taken in and after they entered the hospital, as well as various charts, were hung throughout the meeting venue. In the past six months, 127 helpless children have been taken in, 63 of whom have been selected to enter the educational institutions set up by the association. The rest have been fostered in Xiangshan Orphanage and Taian Orphanage, etc. Chairman Kong Yongzhi, Deputy Chairman Luo Yunyan, and Mrs. Guo Bingwen all had matters and asked for leave, so Executive Committee member Le Lingsheng (transliteration) was elected as chairman. During the opening speech, he spoke in English, which was translated by General Secretary Wu Weide. Then, he reported that from April to December of the 19th year, a total of 29,833.55 yuan was spent on five items: child protection, child education, child health, child research, and social education. Next, Dr. Peter Hui (transliteration), a health expert, gave a speech on child health. Dr. Hui spoke in English, describing the history of child welfare work in the United States in great detail. He held a manuscript in his left hand and a piece of chalk in his right, like a teacher giving a lecture in a school. He spoke and gestured for half an hour, and two Western women recorded with pens and listened attentively, taking it very seriously. After the speech, he smiled and spoke in Chinese, saying that the infant mortality rate in the United States has gradually decreased in recent years. After China pays attention to child health, there will be fewer deaths after birth, and the birth rate should also be considered in terms of population increase. Dr. Hui had been in China for a long time and spoke fluent Chinese. Next, Dr. Chen Heqin, a child education expert, spoke on child education, saying that parental education is the foundation of child education. Children imitate a lot, and the actions of parents unconsciously instill the nature of children. The general parental education in our country is not yet perfect and has a great impact. He gave examples to prove his words and said that being a parent is not easy. The audience laughed. Then, Wang Xiaolai gave a speech, saying that strict fathers and kind mothers are in line with education and cultivation. He dared to say that the children of everyone present are not as numerous as his. This statement caused everyone to laugh. He also said that he had the most children, and after educating the older ones well, the others would follow suit. He cited facts to prove this. He could not remember the names of his dozens of children, so when he came home from work, he ordered them to line up in order, which he did every day. The youngest ones saw that their older brothers and sisters were standing upright in front of him. Although they had just learned to walk and their footing was unstable, they also followed their older siblings and stood still, which showed that children's imitation comes from nature. By analogy, the older ones are well-behaved, and the younger ones learn from them, saving a lot of effort. Finally, he also said that after reading the coffin donation report of Pushan Villa, he learned that an average of 100 children die in Shanghai every day, and most of the origins of the disease are nothing more than excessive hunger and cold, and uneven heating and cooling. If parents can understand the methods of education and cultivation, there would not be so many infant deaths. He hoped that everyone present would expand the publicity of child health methods so that everyone would know, which would be of great merit.

Proving That the Influence of Good and Evil is Connected to the Principle of Wireless Radio 184

— Luxi Layman

Reading the two sentences "easy to agree with the same voice" and "same spirit seeks each other" in books, I thought that the ancients must have had the actual traces of responding and seeking, not just made up empty words. Living in today's world, observing the invention of wireless electricity, I sighed that the principle of responding to requests is in line with it. People ask private words, and heaven hears them like thunder. If people do not believe it, just look at the agility of wireless electricity. Even if separated by thousands of miles, it can knock here and respond there. Experts know that it is because the degree of electrical waves in the air is the same. The degree of good and evil in people's hearts also has the same seat number and different degrees. If goodness and goodness are the same degree, then the reward must be good, and if evil and evil are the same degree, then the reward must be evil. The innumerable thoughts of all beings flow invisibly, like electrical waves traveling through the air, which cannot be seen by the naked eye. Once it encounters the same degree, it will trigger without any error. It can be known that whether it is good or evil is created by the mind. Although the intention is very subtle, it can be magnified without end. The so-called misfortune and fortune have no door, but people invite themselves. No matter whether they are wise or foolish, those who understand this principle can be without a fierce introspection. The villain occasionally feels ashamed that he is not an expert and cannot speak freely, but borrows him to solicit this, and wishes to question all the people in the world who have the mind to seek, promote, and teach the world and the people. Isn't it helpful?

The Supervising Committee Member as Monk in the Control Yuan 185

— By Man Yin

Among the newly appointed supervising committee members of the National Government's Control Yuan, Mr. Xie Wuliang deeply appreciates Zen philosophy and has published works such as "History of Buddhism." His residence in Beijing is called "Compassion Society." His physique resembles the Maitreya Buddha, and his aspirations are always filled with compassion. Consequently, his peers call him "Monk Xie." Following Su Manshu's "Monk Su," there is now also "Monk Xie." However, the Control Yuan's duty is to impeach and investigate, and now "Monk Xie" uses the compassionate gaze of a Bodhisattva to become the fierce glare of a Vajra. Although Wuliang indulges in the joys of Zen, he is ultimately a lay Buddhist. However, it is heard that there is indeed one supervising committee member who practices as a monk, namely, Mr. Ye Quan from Yunnan Province. Ye was originally a brave revolutionary, courageously fighting the enemy, and all who were pointed to by his banner collapsed. However, "one general's success is built upon ten thousand bones turned to dust." From a Buddhist perspective, one ultimately feels the suffering of sentient beings who have encountered this great calamity, which is beyond words. Ye originally had a predestined connection and encountered a wise teacher, a high monk from Mount Emei, who advised him, "The world is turbulent, and the atmosphere of killing pervades the universe. Why does layman also follow and enter the vortex?" Ye explained the difficulty of withdrawing, as the soldiers' loyalty depended entirely on the general, otherwise there would be disintegration. The high monk sighed deeply, "Layman has already broken the precept against killing, so there is nothing that can be done. But you should bravely retreat from the rapid current. The so-called 'lay down the butcher's knife and immediately become a Buddha.'" The layman remembered this. One month and one day, if you see a red light hanging high in the air, do not advance rashly, but immediately rein in your horse and return. Otherwise, you will suffer a fatal disaster. People may be able to advance bravely, but they often cannot retreat bravely. Layman, firmly remember my words." As a result, during a certain battle, Ye Quan was pursuing the enemy in victory, his momentum unstoppable. In the dark night, he suddenly saw a red light in the sky. Ye Quan immediately remembered the high monk's words and immediately ordered the army to retreat. The red light was the enemy's signal. If they had gone deeper, the entire army would have been annihilated. Ye then realized that killing begets killing, and the cycle continues endlessly. He shaved his head, entered the mountains, and took refuge in the emptiness. Although this resembles a myth, the Control Yuan summoned Ye, but they could not find his whereabouts. Ye's inability to take office is no longer in doubt. This monk supervising committee member will remain vacant for a long time.

Indian Travelogue (11) 186

— Linghua

The rhinoceros (Rhinoceroo) is as large as a large ox, with a long face and a single horn in front that is not very large, but its skin is extremely thick and wrinkled, resembling armor and somewhat similar to elephant skin. Its color is ashen gray when in the mud. A mother hippopotamus with a small hippopotamus (Hippotamns), reddish-purple in color, is also as large as the rhinoceros, with a similar face. However, they are still at a distance of twenty or thirty steps when viewed. The method of raising them is also in mud. Their skin is also very thick. I saw a giraffe, which was the first time in my life. According to my research, it should be called a giraffe, which is not wrong. The English name is Giraffe, which is translated as "camel leopard," as its markings resemble those of a leopard, and its species resembles a camel, according to the English name's explanation. However, ancient studies of the giraffe mention a cow's tail, horse's hooves, fleshy horns, and deer's ears, and its shape also matches. Some people also translate it as "long-headed deer," and the deer is a deer-like animal. It is a vegetarian with high moral character. Its head is small and its neck is long, reaching up to eighteen feet. Among all animals, it can look down on everything. The transliteration "giraffe" is likely a native African word. In Africa, they live in herds of thousands, as seen in movies. When the world is united and all nations communicate, it is like the ancient saying, "a auspicious sign of a king." However, this creature has unique skills. Its tongue can thread a needle's eye, and its hooves can kick down a tiger. Its kick is extremely fast, faster than the human eye can blink, and it arrives on the body instantly. Its speed is evident. I believe that this creature must be the giraffe. Therefore, tigers and leopards do not dare to harm this vegetarian animal, so it can lead the beasts. I placed beans in my hand, and it stretched its head to take food from my palm. A Western woman gave it green grass, and it also took it from her palm. Its nature and virtue are similar to that of a deer, without any ferocity. It is docile and gentle, yet capable of subduing tigers and leopards, truly an auspicious creature. There is also a creature similar to a strange monkey (Mandril), shaped like a demon king, frightening, with a red nose, ears, and mouth with patterns, five claws, and a tail and buttocks that are all crimson red. There are also flower-faced small monkeys and long-tailed monkeys, two or three feet long. In general, many animals come from Africa. There are two types of zebras, one with full stripes and one with half stripes. Only the four limbs are striped, and the stripes on the upper body are very few. This is likely due to interbreeding with other species of horses, so the stripes gradually decrease. Zebras are nothing special and resemble donkeys. I gave them beans, and they also took them from my hand. Their smell is very similar to that of donkeys. I find the Chinese idiom "the donkey of Guizhou" very strange, because there are no donkeys in Guizhou and Guangxi. I once asked a person from Guangxi, and they replied that the land is hot, and the donkeys' hooves are thin and cannot withstand the heat, so they cannot be raised. But I do not believe it, because Guangxi is mountainous and the roads are difficult, and all carrying is done by manual labor. If donkeys could be raised, it would greatly reduce the suffering of the people. According to geography, present-day Africa and Egypt are also near the equator, within ten degrees of latitude. Why is it that even before reaching the tropics, donkeys cannot be raised in Guizhou and Guangxi? Yesterday, I read Herbert Spencer's biography, which stated that he often rode donkeys when traveling in Egypt. Why is it that donkeys cannot be raised even before reaching the tropics in Guizhou and Guangxi? I do not believe it. There were large snakes, but I could not see them because the houses were being repaired. Finally, I saw several lions, ashen gray and appearing old and experienced. The males had long manes and were large, while the females were small and without manes. This indicates the natural aggressiveness of the males. South of Annam, tigers are often used to represent power. In India, lions and elephants are preferred. In Western languages, the word for "king" is "lion." Buddha compared himself to a lion's roar. Pictures often depict beautiful women submitting to elephants, which represents the psychology of the expression of power in the natural world.

There are also many women in the park. Aside from a few with the custom of nose piercing, the ordinary Indian women's clothing is somewhat similar to the Guanyin headdress in Chinese paintings, which is very beautiful. However, because Indians are darker due to the heat of the sun, their beauty is ultimately inferior. The wealthy women in Western attire are no less adorned than Western women. Human efforts can surpass nature, and relying solely on nature is insufficient.

Suddenly, a roar erupted, with the force of a mountain valley rushing forth. This is called a lion's roar. I also left the park. The sunlight was shrouded in the evening mist.

Grain 河xia Rice Market Remains Sluggish 197

Zhabei: Yesterday, various firms gradually sold their inventories as the weather cleared up and the end of the month approached, leading to further weakening. Both retailers and bulk buyers adopted a wait-and-see approach. Top-quality white rice was scarce, causing continued market weakness. High-quality rice remained around twelve yuan and a half, with thin but stable sales and sluggish market conditions. Yang Du Jian rice generally weakened, but top-quality rice was slightly stable. The trend toward Yuan-Yin rice continued, keeping prices at a low level. Recently, arrivals in Shanghai have decreased, boosting confidence. Prices fluctuated within a narrow range, with the opening price around twelve yuan.

South Shanghai: Yesterday, it was observed in the Hexia area that the market was sluggish on the 30th. The sluggish sales of white rice from various firms greatly impacted the market, making it difficult to recover. Although there were attempts to stabilize the market in the morning, prices soon declined. Currently, the rice market is facing abundant arrivals from the Yangtze River, poor conditions in the rice markets of producing areas, and large stockpiles in Shanghai, leading to stagnant transactions and weak market conditions. Arrivals of thin early rice from southern firms varied, and sales were slow. Prices have been further reduced, with Yang Du Jian rice and Yuan-Yin rice showing stagnant conditions.

Flour and Wheat Transactions in March 198

Transactions Were Extremely Smooth... but Delivery Quantities Were Very Small

Flour: Yesterday, the total number of flour deliveries for March was only 11,000 bags of Red and Blue Car brands. This small quantity was truly beyond general expectations. Due to falling market prices, only a small number of deliveries took place. It can be seen that the decline was driven by the environment and did not match the actual situation. Most manufacturers gradually withdrew their goods through customer assistance or took them back themselves, resulting in no deliveries. The supply of actual goods is still low, and market prices may slightly increase in mid-April. However, futures trading was very active, almost doubling compared to previous months. Metals Pig Lead Plummets by Forty to Fifty Cash 199

The price of pig lead plummeted yesterday due to a sharp drop of over two pounds in the price of foreign lead. The arrival of Hunan lead in Shanghai further fueled panic throughout the city. Hankou-based Shanghai merchants rushed to sell, causing the standard price to plummet by forty to fifty cash. Currently, Hunan lead is estimated at fifteen taels and three and a half cash, while foreign lead is at sixteen taels and three cash. Transactions were limited to minor purchases by local factories, with virtually no interest from other customers. According to insiders, the sales of pig lead have been very slow recently, and arrivals from various sources continue unabated, maintaining a state of fear. Therefore, there is concern that the trend will continue to weaken in the coming days.

Cotton velour also rose. Liang Wudi brand bright red and concubine colors were both at two cash and one cent. However, plain white had reached two cash and four cents, and Thick Peony brand white muslin was at three cash and three cents. This stable high price is rare. Wool silk cloth is in high demand from the Yangtze River region. Three Horse Head brand was at two taels, eight cash, and two and a half cents, and Three Joint brand was at two taels and seven cash. Flowers Straight Tribute Woolen Cloth from the Hankou region has moved. The Sleeping Dragon Ridge Seven Sons Picture brand is needed at three cash and six and a half cents. Western goods such as plain Western velvet are gradually moving. Taihe Yan Nian brand plain white is at sixteen taels, and Yi Ji brand Three Autumn is at nineteen taels.

Melville Sales Are Sluggish 203

Due to Too High a Selling Price

Melville, specializing in the sale of Western clothing, has qualities known as Hun Tian, Liang Tian, and San Tian, with San Tian being the thickest and most popular. Sales have suddenly become extremely sluggish this spring, reportedly due to the high selling price. Yesterday, Gong Ping, Rong Tai, Zhen Zhi, and TTT Melville sold for three taels and two cash and five cents, while other miscellaneous brands of Chong San Tian sold for only two taels and six or seven cash. The width of Melville is only thirty-two inches. Compared to French flannel, it is extremely uneconomical, as top-quality all-wool French flannel is fifty-eight inches wide and sells for only five taels per yard, while the quality is softer and thicker than Melville. As a result, Melville sales are becoming increasingly sluggish.

Youth Corner

Theft 205

— Guangmei

The affair—theft—although as mundane as eating when hungry and drinking when thirsty, is certainly not as easily encountered in anyone's life history. What is called mundane, needless to say, refers to the entirety of humanity rather than individuals. Of course, there is a segment of people who, due to their lives and circumstances, frequently get to taste it, and naturally, it is nothing to be surprised about for them. However, those who are trying it for the first time cannot avoid adding a few words for the record. At the same time, they feel that although the principles of theft are consistent, the circumstances and methods are not something that can be encompassed in a single statement. Moreover, they have believed throughout the entire theft incident that they were living in a dream world. If they do not take advantage of today's extraordinary impression to leave some traces, they are afraid that it will end up being an unending dream.

The affectionate quilt was still tightly embracing them, each dreaming the beautiful dreams of youthful girls. The lark did not dare to call loudly, fearing to wake them up. The sun had also thoughtfully kept the fact that there were no classes these days in mind, specially hiding its golden face deep in the clouds, so as not to let it shine directly through the window screen onto the dressing table, and then reflected by the mirror directly to their charming faces, disturbing their sleep. At the same time, it did not dare to kiss them lightly, fearing that the lover in their dreams would secretly present them with a silent gun. The alarm clock quietly passed the room while they were still in their dreams. The air was still as quiet as deep night.

"Oh no, the thief has been here, miss..." The nanny cried as she rushed into their room, lifting the bedding to check whether their boxes had been stolen. But her voice was already trembling severely, and her expression was extremely flustered.

In this way, the affection of the quilt, the lark's modesty, and the sun's thoughtfulness were all wasted.

"What, what..." They opened their sleepy eyes as if startled, tilting their short, messy hair. Hearing the nanny crying outside, responding "the thief...", it frightened them.

Then, they saw the fur coat in front of the bed and the coats piled up on the back of the door, declaring their departure.

"We were..." Before they could shout, the nanny cried again, "Also, letters and seals are in the funnel, I don't know whose miss's are..."

"It's mine, and there are things and money too!" Mei heard the seal and letters and knew it was hers, and shouted anxiously, "They are useful things!" Her voice was already trembling with sobs.

"I also have money! The pen should be in there too..."

"All my clothes are gone..."

Ji and Zhi also cried out at the same time. Little Ya, seeing this situation, followed crying. The nanny cried in fear, and the classmates inquired with concern and surprise. Another group of classmates checked their own clothes to see if they had been stolen. And a part of the people were chattering and studying the truth of the theft. "Where did the thief come in from and where did they go out from? It's still snowing, how did they know to only steal from number nine..." For a time, discussions were diverse, crying was noisy. There was the triviality of housewives haggling prices in the small market, the urgency of firefighters rescuing fires in the fire scene, and the lamentations of the stolen. The chaotic air filled the entire girls' dormitory. The place, which was once jokingly called "Palace" by a group of male students, suddenly formed the Hongkou vegetable market.

Other rooms were not involved, only in number nine were found coats, fur coats, silver dollars and other items missing, totaling more than four hundred yuan. The owners were Zhi, Ji and Mei.

Although it was rainy and snowy, the heavens were not beautiful, it was not a problem in Shanghai. They had previously agreed to take advantage of this period without classes to have fun as much as possible, but only limited to the movies. Also, they had been invited early to eat the old calendar New Year's Eve dinner, euphemistically called a gathering. Now, all plans have failed.

Since being stolen from, they have had to stay in their room, unable to go out without clothes.

Strangely, the four coats and other clothes on the back of the door disappeared, and the clothes rack had been replaced with summer clothes. Their own fur coats had turned into velvet-lined coats, and they still had to feel the shivers from time to time. But they still did not believe that their clothes had really been stolen. They were completely like they were dreaming.

Their depression and annoyance, although not a big deal, had other reasons. Ji was originally ill and had not eaten anything for nearly a week. With the added cold, it became more severe. Zhi's fur coat had only been made for six days before it was stolen. She had originally planned to go home for her grandmother's eightieth birthday, but how could she go back now? Her heart was as anxious as a sword. She imagined how much her family was looking forward to her going back, how busy her grandmother's birthday would be. Looking at the current situation, she could only resentfully feel lost. Mei, due to special circumstances, was constantly concerned about her kind mother. Although they had different illnesses, they sympathized with each other.

This was still the first phenomenon. They had changed their usual carefree smiles and noisy attitude. Their liveliness had also disappeared into their sorrow. That clear singing voice could no longer be found in their room. Xiao and the flute could also take advantage of this rare opportunity to rest greatly. Their number nine room, which had always been full of youthful sunshine, had now become a gray, depressed world. The city of sorrow and the sick country had buried them alive.

Gymnastics 206

— Bing She

In recent years, the Jiangwan area will form a school district. In addition to the many schools in Jiangwan, the Faculties of Law, Chi Chih, and Ai Kuo are already standing in a tripartite manner on Jiangwan Road. Recently, each school has experienced theft, and not just once. The local public security bureau has long been troubled by this and feels that the public security is not as quiet. Those responsible for maintaining it were perhaps negligent. The bureau officials were quite clear about the righteousness, so they took this as their fault and shame and decided to solve the case in order to find out about other past theft cases. On the school side, thefts in male and female dormitories were indeed not less than several times.

Since reporting to the Public Security Bureau, the bureau's investigation team has come to inspect the victims' rooms three or four times. Number nine was probably examined as a route for the thief to enter and exit. They felt strange and peculiar. The word "strange" existed in their minds at all times, and even newspaper reporters picked it up and a message was sent by the news agency. They inadvertently discovered the news of their theft in major newspapers, not to mention the tabloids.

Okay, their work came. Although it was relatively troublesome, they could gain considerable comfort and relief from this trouble. During this period, they would always receive several letters of condolence from local or out-of-town.
